SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"

    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0

) AS t

    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."AppraisalCycleId", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."Status", t0."AppraisalFormId", t0."QuestionId", t0."Id", t0."PerformanceIndicatorId", t0."QuestionText", t0."Status"
FROM (
    SELECT a."Id", a."AppraisalCycleId", a."EmployeeRoleId", a."Status"
    FROM appraisal_form AS a
    WHERE a."AppraisalCycleId" = @__appraisalCycleId_0 AND a."EmployeeRoleId" = @__employeeRoleId_1 AND a."Status" = @__status_2
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a0."AppraisalFormId", a0."QuestionId", q."Id", q."PerformanceIndicatorId", q."QuestionText", q."Status"
    FROM appraisal_form_question AS a0
    INNER JOIN question AS q ON a0."QuestionId" = q."Id"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."AppraisalFormId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."AppraisalFormId", t0."QuestionId"

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

FROM (

    FROM appraisal_form AS a
    WHERE a."AppraisalCycleId" = @__appraisalCycleId_0 AND a."EmployeeRoleId" = @__employeeRoleId_1 AND a."Status" = @__status_2
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a0."AppraisalFormId", a0."QuestionId", q."Id", q."PerformanceIndicatorId", q."QuestionText", q."Status"
    FROM appraisal_form_question AS a0
    INNER JOIN question AS q ON a0."QuestionId" = q."Id"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."AppraisalFormId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."AppraisalFormId", t0."QuestionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."AppraisalCycleId", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."Status", t0."AppraisalFormId", t0."QuestionId", t0."Id", t0."PerformanceIndicatorId", t0."QuestionText", t0."Status"
FROM (
    SELECT a."Id", a."AppraisalCycleId", a."EmployeeRoleId", a."Status"
    FROM appraisal_form AS a
    WHERE a."AppraisalCycleId" = @__appraisalCycleId_0 AND a."EmployeeRoleId" = @__employeeRoleId_1 AND a."Status" = @__status_2
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a0."AppraisalFormId", a0."QuestionId", q."Id", q."PerformanceIndicatorId", q."QuestionText", q."Status"
    FROM appraisal_form_question AS a0
    INNER JOIN question AS q ON a0."QuestionId" = q."Id"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."AppraisalFormId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."AppraisalFormId", t0."QuestionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

2024-12-23 18:57:46.131 +05:30 [INF] Executed DbCommand (4ms) [Parameters=[@__email_0='?'], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
